lives entirely under the staging/src/k8s.io/client-go/ directory, which is the canonical source for the published k8s.io/client-go module.\\n\\n## Core cache and sync infrastructure (tools/cache)\\n\\n- **shared_informer.go**: Defines `SharedInformer` and `SharedIndexInformer` interfaces, the `sharedIndexInformer` struct that wires together the Controller+DeltaFIFO+store pipeline, `WaitForCacheSync`/`WaitForNamedCacheSync` for blocking until the local cache is in sync with the API server.\\n- **controller.go**: The `Controller` type that drives a Reflector→DeltaFIFO→store loop. `NewInformer` and `NewIndexerInformer` are the lower-level constructors.\\n- **reflector.go**: `Reflector` implements the list-watch loop: calls `ListWatch.List` to do an initial bulk load, then `ListWatch.Watch` to stream delta events, populating the DeltaFIFO queue.\\n- **listwatch.go**: `ListWatch` struct and `NewListWatchFromClient` — the concrete ListerWatcher backed by a REST client that issues List and Watch API calls to the Kubernetes API server.\\n- **store.go**: `Store` and `Indexer` interfaces; `cache` struct (thread-safe store backed by `threadSafeMap`) is the local in-memory cache.\\n- **thread_safe_store.go**: `ThreadSafeStore` — the low-level concurrent map used by the cache store.\\n- **delta_fifo.go**: `DeltaFIFO` — the FIFO queue that buffers Add/Update/Delete/Sync/Replace events from the Reflector before they are processed into the store.\\n- **index.go**: `Indexer` interface and `MetaNamespaceIndexFunc` helper.\\n- **listers.go**: `GenericLister`/`GenericNamespaceLister` helpers used by typed listers.\\n- **fifo.go**: Classic `FIFO` queue (used by some controllers directly).\\n- **heap.go**: Heap-based priority queue (used by expiration cache).\\n- **object-names.go**: Helpers for extracting object keys.\\n- **mutation_cache.go / mutation_detector.go**: Optional overlay cache for optimistic mutation tracking.\\n- **undelta_store.go**: `UndeltaStore` wraps a store to re-list objects on each event.\\n- **expiration_cache.go / expiration_cache_fakes.go / fake_custom_store.go**: Expiration-aware cache implementations.\\n- **reflector_metrics.go / reflector_data_consistency_detector.go**: Metrics and data-consistency helpers for the Reflector.\\n- **retry_with_deadline.go**: Utility for retrying with a deadline used by the Reflector.\\n- **synctrack/synctrack.go / synctrack/lazy.go**: `AsyncTracker` and `Lazy` — fine-grained per-item sync-state tracking used by sharedIndexInformer to implement `HasSynced`.\\n\\n## SharedInformerFactory (informers/)\\n\\n- **informers/factory.go**: Main `SharedInformerFactory` interface + `sharedInformerFactory` struct. Provides `NewSharedInformerFactory`, `NewSharedInformerFactoryWithOptions`, `InformerFor` (which registers and caches informers by type), `Start` (launches goroutines), and `WaitForCacheSync`.\\n- **informers/generic.go**: `ForResource` method on the factory — dispatches to the correct typed informer by GVR.\\n- **informers/internalinterfaces/factory_interfaces.go**: `SharedInformerFactory` mini-interface (just `Start` + `InformerFor`) used internally to avoid import cycles; `NewInformerFunc` type alias.\\n- **informers/doc.go**: Package documentation.\\n\\n## Dynamic and Metadata informers\\n\\n- **dynamic/dynamicinformer/informer.go + interface.go**: `DynamicSharedInformerFactory` for unstructured dynamic resources.\\n- **metadata/metadatainformer/informer.go + interface.go**: `metadataSharedInformerFactory` for partial-metadata-only informers.\\n\\n## Per-resource informer registrations (informers/{group}/{version}/{resource}.go)\\n\\nEach file under `informers/admissionregistration/`, `informers/apps/`, `informers/autoscaling/`, `informers/batch/`, `informers/certificates/`, `informers/coordination/`, `informers/core/`, `informers/discovery/`, `informers/events/`, `informers/extensions/`, `informers/flowcontrol/`, `informers/networking/`, `informers/node/`, `informers/policy/`, `informers/rbac/`, `informers/resource/`, `informers/scheduling/`, `informers/storage/`, and `informers/storagemigration/` registers one Kubernetes resource type with the factory via `factory.InformerFor(obj, newFunc)`, where `newFunc` calls `NewFilteredXxxInformer` which builds a `ListWatch` from the typed client and constructs a `NewSharedIndexInformer`.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":1,"cache_creation_input_tokens":224,"cache_read_input_tokens":61828,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":224,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":0},"output_tokens":8,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"bf170f96-1b73-49b6-b54b-79ad91297f83","uuid":"259ece50-a21e-4b02-a9b8-adfd20924f4e"}

lives entirely under the staging/src/k8s.io/client-go/ directory, which is the canonical source for the published k8s.io/client-go module.\\n\\n## Core cache and sync infrastructure (tools/cache)\\n\\n- **shared_informer.go**: Defines SharedInformer and SharedIndexInformer interfaces, the sharedIndexInformer struct that wires together the Controller+DeltaFIFO+store pipeline, WaitForCacheSync/WaitForNamedCacheSync for blocking until the local cache is in sync with the API server.\\n- **controller.go**: The Controller type that drives a Reflector->DeltaFIFO->store loop. NewInformer and NewIndexerInformer are the lower-level constructors.\\n- **reflector.go**: Reflector implements the list-watch loop: calls ListWatch.List to do an initial bulk load, then ListWatch.Watch to stream delta events, populating the DeltaFIFO queue.\\n- **listwatch.go**: ListWatch struct and NewListWatchFromClient -- the concrete ListerWatcher backed by a REST client that issues List and Watch API calls to the Kubernetes API server.\\n- **store.go**: Store and Indexer interfaces; cache struct (thread-safe store backed by threadSafeMap) is the local in-memory cache.\\n- **thread_safe_store.go**: ThreadSafeStore -- the low-level concurrent map used by the cache store.\\n- **delta_fifo.go**: DeltaFIFO -- the FIFO queue that buffers Add/Update/Delete/Sync/Replace events from the Reflector before they are processed into the store.\\n- **index.go**: Indexer interface and MetaNamespaceIndexFunc helper.\\n- **listers.go**: GenericLister/GenericNamespaceLister helpers used by typed listers.\\n- **fifo.go**: Classic FIFO queue.\\n- **heap.go**: Heap-based priority queue.\\n- **object-names.go**: Helpers for extracting object keys.\\n- **mutation_cache.go / mutation_detector.go**: Optional overlay cache for optimistic mutation tracking.\\n- **undelta_store.go**: UndeltaStore wraps a store to re-list objects on each event.\\n- **expiration_cache.go / expiration_cache_fakes.go / fake_custom_store.go**: Expiration-aware cache implementations.\\n- **reflector_metrics.go / reflector_data_consistency_detector.go**: Metrics and data-consistency helpers for the Reflector.\\n- **retry_with_deadline.go**: Utility for retrying with a deadline used by the Reflector.\\n- **synctrack/synctrack.go / synctrack/lazy.go**: AsyncTracker and Lazy -- fine-grained per-item sync-state tracking used by sharedIndexInformer to implement HasSynced.\\n\\n## SharedInformerFactory (informers/)\\n\\n- **informers/factory.go**: Main SharedInformerFactory interface + sharedInformerFactory struct. lives entirely under the staging/src/k8s.io/client-go/ directory, which is the canonical source for the published k8s.io/client-go module.\\n\\n## Core cache and sync infrastructure (tools/cache)\\n\\n- **shared_informer.go**: Defines SharedInformer and SharedIndexInformer interfaces, the sharedIndexInformer struct that wires together the Controller+DeltaFIFO+store pipeline, WaitForCacheSync/WaitForNamedCacheSync for blocking until the local cache is in sync with the API server.\\n- **controller.go**: The Controller type that drives a Reflector->DeltaFIFO->store loop. NewInformer and NewIndexerInformer are the lower-level constructors.\\n- **reflector.go**: Reflector implements the list-watch loop: calls ListWatch.List to do an initial bulk load, then ListWatch.Watch to stream delta events, populating the DeltaFIFO queue.\\n- **listwatch.go**: ListWatch struct and NewListWatchFromClient -- the concrete ListerWatcher backed by a REST client that issues List and Watch API calls to the Kubernetes API server.\\n- **store.go**: Store and Indexer interfaces; cache struct (thread-safe store backed by threadSafeMap) is the local in-memory cache.\\n- **thread_safe_store.go**: ThreadSafeStore -- the low-level concurrent map used by the cache store.\\n- **delta_fifo.go**: DeltaFIFO -- the FIFO queue that buffers Add/Update/Delete/Sync/Replace events from the Reflector before they are processed into the store.\\n- **index.go**: Indexer interface and MetaNamespaceIndexFunc helper.\\n- **listers.go**: GenericLister/GenericNamespaceLister helpers used by typed listers.\\n- **fifo.go**: Classic FIFO queue.\\n- **heap.go**: Heap-based priority queue.\\n- **object-names.go**: Helpers for extracting object keys.\\n- **mutation_cache.go / mutation_detector.go**: Optional overlay cache for optimistic mutation tracking.\\n- **undelta_store.go**: UndeltaStore wraps a store to re-list objects on each event.\\n- **expiration_cache.go / expiration_cache_fakes.go / fake_custom_store.go**: Expiration-aware cache implementations.\\n- **reflector_metrics.go / reflector_data_consistency_detector.go**: Metrics and data-consistency helpers for the Reflector.\\n- **retry_with_deadline.go**: Utility for retrying with a deadline used by the Reflector.\\n- **synctrack/synctrack.go / synctrack/lazy.go**: AsyncTracker and Lazy -- fine-grained per-item sync-state tracking used by sharedIndexInformer to implement HasSynced.\\n\\n## SharedInformerFactory (informers/)\\n\\n- **informers/factory.go**: Main SharedInformerFactory interface + sharedInformerFactory struct. Provides NewSharedInformerFactory, NewSharedInformerFactoryWithOptions, InformerFor (registers and caches informers by type), Start (launches goroutines), and WaitForCacheSync.\\n- **informers/generic.go**: ForResource method -- dispatches to the correct typed informer by GVR.\\n- **informers/internalinterfaces/factory_interfaces.go**: SharedInformerFactory mini-interface (just Start + InformerFor) used internally to avoid import cycles; NewInformerFunc type alias.\\n- **informers/doc.go**: Package documentation.\\n\\n## Dynamic and Metadata informers\\n\\n- **dynamic/dynamicinformer/informer.go + interface.go**: DynamicSharedInformerFactory for unstructured dynamic resources.\\n- **metadata/metadatainformer/informer.go + interface.go**: metadataSharedInformerFactory for partial-metadata-only informers.\\n\\n## Per-resource informer registrations (informers/{group}/{version}/{resource}.go)\\n\\nEach file under informers/admissionregistration/, informers/apps/, informers/autoscaling/, informers/batch/, informers/certificates/, informers/coordination/, informers/core/, informers/discovery/, informers/events/, informers/extensions/, informers/flowcontrol/, informers/networking/, informers/node/, informers/policy/, informers/rbac/, informers/resource/, informers/scheduling/, informers/storage/, and informers/storagemigration/ registers one Kubernetes resource type with the factory via factory.InformerFor(obj, newFunc), where newFunc calls NewFilteredXxxInformer which builds a ListWatch from the typed client and constructs a NewSharedIndexInformer.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
